You will take seminars on the second-year undergraduate module ‘Galleons and Caravans: Global Connection 1300-1800’ and you will take seminars on one other undergraduate module, most likely ‘The European World.’ Your teaching will amount to a total of nine seminar groups of approximately fourteen students per group.
